<li><strong>Reliable agents</strong>: Built on ground truth data for consistent, trustworthy results.</li>
<li><strong>Controllable output</strong>: Tailor output with flexible constraints to fit your needs.</li>
<li><strong>Specialized in data processing</strong>: Agents excel in custom data labeling and processing tasks.</li>
<li><strong>Autonomous learning</strong>: Agents evolve through observations and reflections, not just automation.</li>
<li><strong>Flexible and extensible runtime</strong>: Adaptable framework with community-driven evolution for diverse needs.</li>
<li><strong>Easily customizable</strong>: Develop agents swiftly for unique challenges, no steep learning curve.</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/LehengTHU/Agent4Rec"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">Agent4Rec</font></font></a></h2><a id="user-content-agent4rec" class="anchor" aria-label="永久链接：Agent4Rec" href="#agent4rec"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">具有 1,000 个代理的推荐系统模拟器</font></font></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">General purpose, Build your own, Multi-agent</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Agent4Rec is a recommender system simulator that utilizes 1,000 LLM-empowered generative agents.</li>
<li>These agents are initialized from the <a href="https://grouplens.org/datasets/movielens/1m/" rel="nofollow">MovieLens-1M</a> dataset, embodying varied social traits and preferences.</li>
<li>Each agent interacts with personalized movie recommendations in a page-by-page manner and undertakes various actions such as watching, rating, evaluating, exiting, and interviewing.</li>
</ul>

<p dir="auto">General purpose, Build your own, Multi-agent</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-2" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A low-code framework designed for the swift creation, testing, and iteration of AI-powered autonomous agents and Cognitive Architectures, compatible with various LLM models.</li>
<li>Facilitates building custom agents and cognitive architectures with ease.</li>
<li>Supports multiple LLM models including OpenAI, Anthropic's Claude, and local Oobabooga, allowing flexibility in running different models for different agents based on specific requirements.</li>
<li>Provides customizable agent memory management and on-the-fly prompt editing for rapid development and testing.</li>
<li>Comes with a database-agnostic design ensuring seamless extensibility, with straightforward integration with different databases like ChromaDB for various AI projects.</li>
</ul>

<p dir="auto">General purpose</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-3" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A no-code platform</li>
<li>Process:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Assigning a goal to the agent</li>
<li>Witnessing its thinking process</li>
<li>Formulation of an execution plan</li>
<li>Taking actions accordingly</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Uses OpenAI functions</li>
<li>Supports gpt-3.5-16k, pinecone and pg_vector databases</li>
<li>Stack
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Frontend: NextJS + Typescript</li>
<li>Backend: FastAPI + Python</li>
<li>DB: MySQL through docker with the option of running SQLite locally</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/aiwaves-cn/agents"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">代理商</font></font></a></h2><a id="user-content-agents" class="anchor" aria-label="永久链接： 代理" href="#agents"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">用于构建语言代理的库/框架</font></font></p>
<details>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://github.com/aiwaves-cn/agents/raw/master/assets/agents-logo.png"><img src="https://github.com/aiwaves-cn/agents/raw/master/assets/agents-logo.png" alt="Image" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-5" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-5"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">General purpose, Build your own, Multi-agent</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-5" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-5"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Long-short Term Memory</strong>: Language agents in the library are equipped with both long-term memory implemented via VectorDB + Semantic Search and short-term memory (working memory) maintained and updated by an LLM.</li>
<li><strong>Tool Usage</strong>: Language agents in the library can use any external tools via  <a href="https://platform.openai.com/docs/guides/gpt/function-calling" rel="nofollow">function-calling</a>  and developers can add customized tools/APIs  <a href="https://github.com/aiwaves-cn/agents/blob/master/src/agents/Component/ToolComponent.py">here</a>.</li>
<li><strong>Web Navigation</strong>: Language agents in the library can use search engines to navigate the web and get useful information.</li>
<li><strong>Multi-agent Communication</strong>: In addition to single language agents, the library supports building multi-agent systems in which language agents can communicate with other language agents and the environment. Different from most existing frameworks for multi-agent systems that use pre-defined rules to control the order for agents' action,  <strong>Agents</strong>  includes a  <em>controller</em>  function that dynamically decides which agent will perform the next action using an LLM by considering the previous actions, the environment, and the target of the current states. This makes multi-agent communication more flexible.</li>
<li><strong>Human-Agent interaction</strong>: In addition to letting language agents communicate with each other in an environment, our framework seamlessly supports human users to play the role of the agent by himself/herself and input his/her own actions, and interact with other language agents in the environment.</li>
<li><strong>Symbolic Control</strong>: Different from existing frameworks for language agents that only use a simple task description to control the entire multi-agent system over the whole task completion process,  <strong>Agents</strong>  allows users to use an  <strong>SOP (Standard Operation Process)</strong>  that defines subgoals/subtasks for the overall task to customize fine-grained workflows for the language agents.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Links</h3><a id="user-content-links-5" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Links" href="#links-5"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-8" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-8"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Aider is a command line tool that lets you pair program with GPT-3.5/GPT-4, to edit code stored in your local git repository</li>
<li>You can start a new project or work with an existing repo. And you can fluidly switch back and forth between the aider chat where you ask GPT to edit the code and your own editor to make changes yourself</li>
<li>Aider makes sure edits from you and GPT are committed to git with sensible commit messages. Aider is unique in that it works well with pre-existing, larger codebases</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-10" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-10"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A framework for developing LLM (Large Language Model) applications with multiple conversational agents.</li>
<li>These agents can collaborate to solve tasks and can interact seamlessly with humans.</li>
<li>It simplifies complex LLM workflows, enhancing automation and optimization.</li>
<li>It offers a range of working systems across various domains and complexities.</li>
<li>It improves LLM inference with easy performance tuning and utility features like API unification and caching.</li>
<li>It supports advanced usage patterns, including error handling, multi-config inference, and context programming.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Links</h3><a id="user-content-links-10" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Links" href="#links-10"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Paper: <a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/2308.08155.pdf" rel="nofollow">AutoGen: Enabling Next-Gen LLM Applications via Multi-Agent Conversation Framework</a></li>

</ul>
</details>

<p dir="auto">General purpose</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-11" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-11"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>An experimental open-source attempt to make GPT-4 fully autonomous, with &gt;140k stars on GitHub</li>
<li>Chains together LLM "thoughts", to autonomously achieve whatever goal you set</li>
<li>Internet access for searches and information gathering</li>
<li>Long-term and short-term memory management</li>
<li>Can execute many commands such as Google Search, browse websites, write to files, and execute Python files and much more</li>
<li>GPT-4 instances for text generation</li>
<li>Access to popular websites and platforms</li>
<li>File storage and summarization with GPT-3.5</li>
<li>Extensibility with Plugins</li>
<li>"A lot like BabyAGI combined with LangChain tools"</li>
<li>Features added in release 0.4.0
<ul dir="auto">
<li>File reading</li>
<li>Commands customization</li>
<li>Enhanced testing</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>Model: GPT 4</li>
<li>Automata takes your project as a context, receives tasks, and executes the instructions seamlessly.</li>
<li>Features
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Automata aims to evolve into a fully autonomous, self-programming Artificial Intelligence system.</li>
<li>It's designed for seamless integration with all available agent platforms and LLM providers.</li>
<li>Utilizes the novel code search algorithm, SymbolRank, and associated tools to build superior coding intelligence.</li>
<li>Modular, fully configurable design with minimal reliance on external dependencies</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>A prototype enterprise application - an Autonomous HR Assistant powered by GPT-3.5.</li>
<li>An agent that can answer HR related queries autonomously using the tools it has on hand.</li>
<li>Powered by GPT-3.5</li>
<li>Current tools assigned to the agent (with more on the way):
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Timekeeping Policy</li>
<li>Employee Data</li>
<li>Calculator</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">使用人工智能管理任务的简单框架</font></font></p>
<details>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/21254008/235015461-543a897f-70cc-4b63-941a-2ae3c9172b11.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/21254008/235015461-543a897f-70cc-4b63-941a-2ae3c9172b11.png" alt="Image" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-15" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-15"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">General purpose</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-15" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-15"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A pared-down version of the original <a href="https://twitter.com/yoheinakajima/status/1640934493489070080?s=20" rel="nofollow">Task-Driven Autonomous Agent</a></li>
<li>Creates tasks based on the result of previous tasks and a predefined objective.</li>
<li>The script then uses OpenAI's NLP capabilities to create new tasks based on the objective</li>
<li>Leverages OpenAI's GPT-4, pinecone vector search, and LangChainAI framework</li>
<li>Default model is OpenAI GPT3-turbo</li>
<li>The system maintains a task list for managing and prioritizing tasks</li>
<li>It autonomously creates new tasks based on completed results and reprioritizes the task list accordingly, showcasing the adaptability of AI-powered language models</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Links</h3><a id="user-content-links-15" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Links" href="#links-15"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<p dir="auto">General purpose, Productivity</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-16" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-16"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A more advanced version of the original BabyAGI code</li>
<li>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Improves upon the original framework, by introducing a more complex task management prompt, allowing for more comprehensive analysis and synthesis of information</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Designed to handle multiple functions within one task management prompt</li>
<li>Built on top of the GPT-4 architecture, resulting in slower processing speeds and occasional errors</li>
<li>Provides a framework that can be further built upon and improved, paving the way for more sophisticated AI applications</li>
<li>One of the significant differences between BabyAGI and BabyBeeAGI is the complexity of the task management prompt</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://replit.com/@YoheiNakajima/BabyCatAGI" rel="nofollow"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">猫宝宝AGI</font></font></a></h2><a id="user-content-babycatagi" class="anchor" aria-label="永久链接：BabyCatAGI" href="#babycatagi"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">BabyCatAGI 是 BabyBeeAGI 的一个模组</font></font></p>
<details>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/c7ce68f851c724e27e1e9cf0a1b2fb11a4dd22e3bda4ee3d69040d1a43edab58/68747470733a2f2f7062732e7477696d672e636f6d2f6d656469612f467742776f527261634149393969503f666f726d61743d6a7067266e616d653d6d656469756d"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/c7ce68f851c724e27e1e9cf0a1b2fb11a4dd22e3bda4ee3d69040d1a43edab58/68747470733a2f2f7062732e7477696d672e636f6d2f6d656469612f467742776f527261634149393969503f666f726d61743d6a7067266e616d653d6d656469756d" alt="Image" data-canonical-src="https://pbs.twimg.com/media/FwBwoRracAI99iP?format=jpg&amp;name=medium" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-17" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-17"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">General purpose</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-17" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-17"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Just 300 lines of code</li>
<li>This was built as a d iteration on the original BabyAGI code in a lightweight way. Differences to BabyAGI include the following:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Task Creation Agent runs once</li>
<li>Execution Agent loops through tasks</li>
<li>Task dependencies for pulling relevant results</li>
<li>Two tools: search tool and text completion</li>
<li>“Mini-agent” as tool</li>
<li>Search tool combines search, scrape, chunking, and extraction.</li>
<li>Results combined to create summary report</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/saten-private/BabyCommandAGI"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">宝贝指挥AGI</font></font></a></h2><a id="user-content-babycommandagi" class="anchor" aria-label="永久链接：BabyCommandAGI" href="#babycommandagi"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">测试将 CLI 和 LLM 结合起来会发生什么</font></font></p>
<details>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://github.com/saten-private/BabyCommandAGI/raw/main/docs/Architecture.png"><img src="https://github.com/saten-private/BabyCommandAGI/raw/main/docs/Architecture.png" alt="Image" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-21" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-21"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">General purpose, Coding</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-20" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-20"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>gent designed to test what happens when you combine CLI and LLM, which are more traditional interfaces than GUI (created by @saten-private)</li>
<li>An AI agent based on @yoheinakajima's <a href="https://github.com/yoheinakajima/babyagi">BabyAGI</a> which executes shell commands</li>
<li>Automatic Programming, Successfully created an app automatically just by providing feedback. The procedure can be found <a href="https://twitter.com/saten_work/status/1674855573412810753" rel="nofollow">here</a>.</li>
<li>Automatic Environment Setup, Successfully installed a Flutter environment on Linux in a container, created the Flutter app, and launched it. The procedure can be found <a href="https://twitter.com/saten_work/status/1667126272072491009" rel="nofollow">here</a>.</li>
<li>Aside from setting up the environment, it seems to be able to handle a bit of general tasks such as <a href="https://anyaitools.com/babycommandagi/?utm_source=SocialAutoPoster&amp;utm_medium=Social&amp;utm_campaign=Twitter" rel="nofollow">Generating text, like poems, code, scripts, musical pieces, email, and letters, translating languages</a></li>
<li>There is a risk of breaking the environment. Please run in a virtual environment such as Docker.</li>
<li>GPT-4 or higher is recommended</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Links</h3><a id="user-content-links-20" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Links" href="#links-20"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yoheinakajima/babyagi/tree/main/classic/babyfoxagi"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">狐狸宝宝AGI</font></font></a></h2><a id="user-content-babyfoxagi" class="anchor" aria-label="永久链接：BabyFoxAGI" href="#babyfoxagi"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">BabyAGI 模组，带有新的并行 UI 面板</font></font></p>
<details>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/adac5489348b4847f2fac45d3904ef4c39e33a7355f31842a3b1a52ec0e541a0/68747470733a2f2f7062732e7477696d672e636f6d2f6d656469612f4632567074344562494141613332363f666f726d61743d6a7067266e616d653d6d656469756d"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/adac5489348b4847f2fac45d3904ef4c39e33a7355f31842a3b1a52ec0e541a0/68747470733a2f2f7062732e7477696d672e636f6d2f6d656469612f4632567074344562494141613332363f666f726d61743d6a7067266e616d653d6d656469756d" alt="Image" data-canonical-src="https://pbs.twimg.com/media/F2Vpt4EbIAAa326?format=jpg&amp;name=medium" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-22" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-22"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">General purpose</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-21" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-21"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A mod of BabyElfAGI, in a series of mods w the naming of BabyAGI in alphabetical order</li>
<li>Self-improving task lists (FOXY method)
<ul dir="auto">
<li>By storing a final reflection at the end, and pulling the most relevant reflection to guide future runs, BabyAGI slowly generates better and better tasks lists</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Novel Chat UI w parallel tasks
<ul dir="auto">
<li>You can chat w BabyAGI! It has an experimental UI where the chat is separate from the tasks/output panel, allowing you to request multiple tasks in parallel</li>
<li>The Chat UI can use a single skill quickly, or chain multiple skills together using a tasklist</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>New skills
<ul dir="auto">
<li>🎨 DALLE skill with prompt assist</li>
<li>🎶 Music player w Deezer</li>
<li>📊 Airtable search (add your own table/base ID)</li>
<li>🔍 Startup Analyst (example of beefy function call as a skill)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>It’s own README</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/pgalko/BambooAI"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">竹艾</font></font></a></h2><a id="user-content-bambooai" class="anchor" aria-label="永久链接：BambooAI" href="#bambooai"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">面向非程序员的数据探索和分析</font></font></p>
<details>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/80b411910c4a6d66dd8d43d2f530f884f2eb71b76b5e23479a9c7a4b87c0e80e/68747470733a2f2f7062732e7477696d672e636f6d2f636172645f696d672f313734353138373733343630323331333733302f662d57356b6249553f666f726d61743d6a7067266e616d653d6d656469756d"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/80b411910c4a6d66dd8d43d2f530f884f2eb71b76b5e23479a9c7a4b87c0e80e/68747470733a2f2f7062732e7477696d672e636f6d2f636172645f696d672f313734353138373733343630323331333733302f662d57356b6249553f666f726d61743d6a7067266e616d653d6d656469756d" alt="Image" data-canonical-src="https://pbs.twimg.com/card_img/1745187734602313730/f-W5kbIU?format=jpg&amp;name=medium" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-23" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-23"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Data analysis</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-22" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-22"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>BambooAI runs in a loop (until user decides to end it).</li>
<li>Allows mixing of different models with different capabilities, token costs and context windows for different tasks.</li>
<li>Maintains the memory of previous conversations.</li>
<li>Builds the prompts dynamically utilising relevant context from Pinecone vector DB.</li>
<li>Offers a narrative or asks follow up questions if required.</li>
<li>For codified responses, the task is broken down into a list of steps and a pseudo-code algorithm is built.</li>
<li>Based on the algorithm, it ises the python code for dataset analysis, modeling or plotting.</li>
<li>Debugs the code which then executes, auto-corrects if needs to, and displays the output to user.</li>
<li>Ranks the final answers, and asks user for feedback.</li>
<li>Builds a vector DB knowledge-base, based on the rank and the user feedback.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Links</h3><a id="user-content-links-22" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Links" href="#links-22"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">适用于广泛任务的早期项目</font></font></p>

<p dir="auto">Coding</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-24" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-24"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A GPT-4 powered semantic code search engine that uses an AI agent</li>
<li>Precise code navigation</li>
<li>Built on stack graphs and scope queries</li>
<li>Fast code search and regex matching engine written in Rust</li>
<li>Allows to find Code on Rust and Typescript</li>
<li>Allows to stage changes</li>
<li>The agent searches both your local and remote repositories with natural language, regex and filtered queries</li>
<li>Bloop can be run via app (easy to download via GitHub)</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-25" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-25"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A highly capable, autonomous AI Agent with an easy to use CLI, RESTful/WebSocket API, Pre-built Docker image and a robust suite of integrated tools.</li>
<li>Support for all GPT-N, Embeddings and Dall-E OpenAI Models</li>
<li>Support for Azure OpenAI Services</li>
<li>Easy to use SDK for integration into any application</li>
<li>Powerful <strong>Code Interpreter</strong> capabilities</li>
<li>Powerful data query capabilities via Postgres DB integration</li>
<li>Pre-built Docker image provides safe execution environment for code generation/execution</li>
<li>Support for telephony applications (via BlandAI)</li>
<li>Support for stock trading (via Alpaca Markets)</li>
<li>Integrates with Gmail and Google Search</li>
<li>Easy to install <code>pip install bondai</code></li>
<li>To start the CLI just run <code>bondai</code></li>
<li>To start the RESTful/WebSocket API just run <code>bondai --server</code></li>
</ul>

<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">基于 Cal.com 构建的开源调度助手</font></font></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-26" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-26"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Cal.ai can book meetings, summarize your week, and find time with others based on natural language.</li>
<li>Responds flexibly to unseen tasks eg. "move my second-last meeting to tomorrow morning".</li>
<li>Uses GPT-4 and LangChain Agent Executor under the hood.</li>

<p dir="auto">General purpose</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-27" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-27"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>CAMEL is an open-source library designed for the study of autonomous and communicative agents.
1)AI user agent: give instructions to the AI assistant with the goal of completing the task.</li>
</ul>
<ol start="2" dir="auto">
<li>AI assistant agent: follow AI user’s instructions and respond with solutions to the task</li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>CAMEL also has an open-source community dedicated to the study of autonomous and communicative agents</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-29" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-29"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Design, Build-your-own, SDK for AI apps, Multi-agent</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-28" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-28"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>ChatArena (or Chat Arena) is a Multi-Agent Language Game Environments for LLMs. The goal is to develop communication and collaboration capabilities of AIs.
ChatArena provides:</li>
<li>A general framework for building interactive environments for multiple large language models (LLMs).</li>
<li>A collection of pre-built or community-created  environments.</li>
<li>User-friendly interfaces with both Web UI and commandline interfaces.</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-30" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-30"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Coding, Multi-agent</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-29" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-29"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>ChatDev is a virtual software company driven by a multitude of intelligent agents assuming different roles such as CEO, CPO, CTO, programmer, reviewer, tester, and art designer, each represented by unique icons.</li>
<li>These agents collaborate in a structured organizational environment, fulfilling the company's mission to "revolutionize the digital world through programming." They engage in functional seminars focusing on design, coding, testing, and documentation.</li>
<li>ChatDev aims to provide an accessible, modular, and extensible platform based on large language models, facilitating the study of collective intelligence in a controlled setting.</li>
<li>The framework allows for extensive customization, empowering users to tailor the software development process, define phases, and establish specific roles within the virtual company.</li>
<li>ChatDev is committed to open-source principles, encouraging contributions from the community and sharing advancements transparently.</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ur-whitelab/chemcrow-public"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">化学乌鸦</font></font></a></h2><a id="user-content-chemcrow" class="anchor" aria-label="永久链接：ChemCrow" href="#chemcrow"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">LangChain 化学相关任务代理</font></font></p>
<details>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://github.com/ur-whitelab/chemcrow-public/raw/main/assets/chemcrow_dark_bold.png"><img src="https://github.com/ur-whitelab/chemcrow-public/raw/main/assets/chemcrow_dark_bold.png" alt="Image" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-31" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-31"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Science, Chemistry</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-30" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-30"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>ChemCrow is an open source package for the accurate solution of reasoning-intensive chemical tasks</li>
<li>It integrates 13 expert-design tools to augment LLM performance in chemistry and demonstrate effectiveness in automating chemical tasks</li>
<li>Built with Langchain</li>
<li>The LLM is provided with a list of tool names, descriptions of their utility, and details about the expected input/output. It is then instructed to answer a user-given prompt using the tools provided when necessary. The instruction suggests the model to follow the ReAct format - Thought, Action, Action Input, Observation. One interesting observation is that while the LLM-based evaluation concluded that GPT-4 and ChemCrow perform nearly equivalently, human evaluations with experts oriented towards the completion and chemical correctness of the solutions showed that ChemCrow outperforms GPT-4 by a large margin. This indicates a potential problem with using LLM to evaluate its own performance on domains that requires deep expertise. The lack of expertise may cause LLMs not knowing its flaws and thus cannot well judge the correctness of task results. (Source: <a href="https://lilianweng.github.io/posts/2023-06-23-agent/" rel="nofollow">Weng, Lilian. (Jun 2023). LLM-powered Autonomous Agents". Lil’Log. https://lilianweng.github.io/posts/2023-06-23-agent/.</a>)</li>
</ul>

<li>It can plan, write, debug, and test some projects autonomously.</li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-32" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-32"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>An intelligent assistant serving the entire software development lifecycle, powered by a Multi-Agent Framework, working with DevOps Toolkits, Code&amp;Doc Repo RAG, etc.</li>
</ul>

<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">编排角色扮演代理的框架</font></font></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-37" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-37"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Build-your-own, SDK for agents, Multi-agent</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-36" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-36"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Cutting-edge framework for orchestrating role-playing, autonomous AI agents.</li>
<li>By fostering collaborative intelligence, CrewAI empowers agents to work together seamlessly, tackling complex tasks.</li>
<li>Crew AI is a multi-agent framework built on LangChain, aiming to empower engineers to harness the collective power of AI agents. In contrast to traditional automation methods, Crew AI introduces a new approach to collaborative decision-making, enhanced creativity, and solving complex problems.</li>
<li>The design philosophy of Crew AI advocates simplicity through modularity. Its main components include agents, tools, tasks, processes, and crews. Each agent is akin to a team member, possessing specific roles, background stories, goals, and memories. Through modular design, we make the intricate world of AI agents accessible, manageable, and more engaging.</li>
</ul>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>A super-easy no-code platform for creating AI chatbots trained on your own data</li>

</ul>
</li>

<ul dir="auto">

<li>Load data from anywhere</li>
<li>No-code: User-friendly interface to manage your datastores and chat with your data</li>
<li>Secured API endpoint for querying your data</li>
<li>Auto sync data sources (coming soon)</li>
<li>Auto generates a ChatGPT Plugin for each datastore</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-38" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-38"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>DemoGPT leverages the power of Language Models (LLMs) to provide fast and effective demo creation for applications.</li>
<li>Automates the prototyping process, making it more efficient and saving valuable time.</li>
<li>Understands and processes the given prompts to generate relevant applications.</li>
<li>Integrated with LangChain for generating application code through iterative parsing of LangChain's documentation with a "Tree of Transformations" (ToT) approach.</li>
<li>The roadmap for DemoGPT includes constant updates and improvements based on user feedback and real-world application, working towards refining the technology and solving the hallucination problem.</li>
<li>"We are planning to introduce features that will further enhance the application generation process, making it more user-friendly and efficient."</li>
</ul>

<p dir="auto">Welcome to the AI Driven Software Development Automation Solution, abbreviated as DevOpsGPT. We combine LLM (Large Language Model) with DevOps tools to convert natural language requirements into working software. This innovative feature greatly improves development efficiency, shortens development cycles, and reduces communication costs, resulting in higher-quality software delivery.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Features and Benefits</h3><a id="user-content-features-and-benefits" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Features and Benefits" href="#features-and-benefits"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Improved development efficiency: No need for tedious requirement document writing and explanations. Users can interact directly with DevOpsGPT to quickly convert requirements into functional software.</li>
<li>Shortened development cycles: The automated software development process significantly reduces delivery time, accelerating software deployment and iterations.</li>
<li>Reduced communication costs: By accurately understanding user requirements, DevOpsGPT minimizes the risk of communication errors and misunderstandings, enhancing collaboration efficiency between development and business teams.</li>
<li>High-quality deliverables: DevOpsGPT generates code and performs validation, ensuring the quality and reliability of the delivered software.</li>
<li>[Enterprise Edition] Existing project analysis: Through AI, automatic analysis of existing project information, accurate decomposition and development of required tasks on the basis of existing projects.</li>
<li>[Enterprise Edition] Professional model selection: Support language model services stronger than GPT in the professional field to better complete requirements development tasks, and support private deployment.</li>
<li>[Enterprise Edition] Support more DevOps platforms: can connect with more DevOps platforms to achieve the development and deployment of the whole process.</li>
</ul>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>OC AI based Compiler, for converting english based markdown specs, into functional code</li>
<li>"We know that all great™ projects start with awesome™ detailed functional specifications. Which is typically written in English, or its many other spoken language alternatives.</li>
<li>So what if, instead of writing code from functional specs, we simply compile it directly to code?</li>
<li>Into a future, where we replace nearly everything, with just written text."</li>
</ul>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>What makes evo.ninja special is that it adapts itself in real-time, based on the tasks at hand.</li>
<li>Evo utilizes pre-defined agent personas that are tailored to specific domains of tasks.</li>
<li>Each iteration of evo's execution loop it will select and adopt the persona that fits the task at hand best.</li>
</ul>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>A developer assistant able to make whole nodejs project with unlimited prompts</li>
<li>Provides a core prompt for building the foundation of your application</li>
<li>Allows you to add unlimited sections, each of which is a prompt representing a specific part of your app</li>
<li>Features
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Friday utilizes GPT-4 for AI assistance, but it has been tested and optimized with GPT-4-32k for improved speed and better results.</li>
<li>It requires 2 small requests for your app's base and 1 request per section you provide.</li>
<li>Friday employs esbuild behind the scenes for every app created by it.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-49" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-49"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Coding</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-48" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-48"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">GPT Engineer is an AI agent that generates an entire codebase based on a prompt.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Model: GPT 4</li>
<li>Specify your project, and the AI agent asks for clarification, and then constructs the entire code base</li>
<li>Features
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Made to be easy to adapt, extend, and make your agent learn how you want your code to look. It generates an entire codebase based on a prompt</li>
<li>You can specify the "identity" of the AI agent by editing the files in the identity folder</li>
<li>Editing the identity and evolving the main prompt is currently how you make the agent remember things between projects</li>
<li>Each step in steps.py will have its communication history with GPT4 stored in the logs folder, and can be rerun with scripts/rerun_edited_message_logs.py</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/0xpayne/gpt-migrate"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">GPT 迁移</font></font></a></h2><a id="user-content-gpt-migrate" class="anchor" aria-label="永久链接：GPT 迁移" href="#gpt-migrate"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Category</h3><a id="user-content-category-50" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Category" href="#category-50"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Coding</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-49" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-49"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">GOT Migrate easily migrates your codebase from one framework or language to another.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Pick from different LLMs</li>
<li>Ability to allow GPT Migration to generate and run unit tests for the new codebase</li>
<li>Ability to select source and target language of the migration</li>
<li>Ability to customize the agent's workflow (setup -&gt; migrate -&gt; test)</li>
<li>GPT Migrate team is working on adding <a href="https://github.com/0xpayne/gpt-migrate#-benchmarks">benchmarks</a> for the agent</li>
</ul>

<p dir="auto">Coding</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h3><a id="user-content-description-50" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description-50"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">GPT Pilot is an AI agent that codes the entire app as you oversee the code being written</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Dev tool that writes scalable apps from scratch while the developer oversees the implementation</li>
<li>A research project to see how can GPT-4 be utilized to generate fully working, production-ready, apps</li>
<li>The main idea is that AI can write most of the code for an app (maybe 95%) but for the rest 5%, a developer is and will be needed until we get full AGI</li>
</ul>
